--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
   1- 14 A14    ---      SpName  Spectrum name without spSpec and .fit
  20- 42 A23    ---      Name    SDSS Name
  53- 62 F10.6  deg      RAdeg   Right Ascension in decimal degrees (J2000)
  73- 82 F10.6  deg      DEdeg   Declination in decimal degrees (J2000)

 278-280 A3     ---      Type    Source type; BHB = Blue Horizontal Branch (6)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Note (2): Relative to the continuum at the line core.
